Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Selected Words
66
Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family Association, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
Our Shame
Is there anyone here who has never seen me before? Today, I will speak on the topic of 'Our Shame.'
You all know well that the world we live in has not become an ideal world. You also know that the world we live in is not a world of causes but a world of results. We are not trying to start; rather, we have already started and are going somewhere. However, if the results are good, then the causes and processes will also be good, and if the processes are good, the goals will also be good, and the starting point will also be good.
Living in a Shameful World
When we think about whether we are going through a happy process, we come to realize that we are not. When we consider whether we live in an unhappy world or a happy world, we can surmise that we are closer to an unhappy world than a happy one. In other words, we reach the conclusion that we are not living in a world that we can be proud of, but rather in a world that we should feel ashamed of.
When we look at the fact that we stand in such a position, we cannot help but acknowledge that we started from a fundamentally flawed place. That shame is what kind of shame, and what kind of wrongness that wrongness represents, becomes the issue.
When you think about 'sin,' there are various kinds of sins. There are also various motivations behind shame. If we live in a shameful world and a sinful world, we cannot help but think about what kind of shame and what kind of sin we are dealing with.
If you visit a prison, you will find that the people who are considered the most shameful and the worst are murderers and robbers. Next are traitors. We cannot help but think about what comes next.
Here, the relationship centered on love is the issue. It is a problem that arises from not engaging in principled love but rather committing acts like rape or coercive love. If we focus on the issue of love, there must be an order of love, and if that order is turned upside down, such as having an affair with one's sister or having some kind of relationship with one's aunt or mother, it becomes an unspeakable shame.
If there is such a reversed relationship in the matter of love, it is something that cannot be spoken of. Such a situation is more despised than murderers and robbers, and that is the reality of prison life. If you go to places like prisons, you will surely feel this.
The Content of the Shame Committed by the First Human Ancestors and God's Position
So when we say that we have become unhappy in this world, the question is why we have become unhappy. It is because we have committed sins or because we have stood in shameful positions. There is no other reason for unhappiness.
From that perspective, as we learn the principles, when we think about our human ancestors again, we can surmise what kind of sins they committed and what kind of shameful positions they were in. Whether we look at Eve or Adam or the archangel...
The archangel killed Eve and Adam. Then Eve brought Adam into a position where he would die. As this lineage of sin began, what happened? They entered into an adulterous love relationship.
So what kind of love relationship was that? We need to examine it. What kind of love relationship was it? It should have been in the order of God, Adam, Eve, and the archangel, but it was reversed to archangel, Eve, Adam, and God. From the archangel's perspective, who were Adam and Eve? They were the masters. Therefore, having a relationship with Eve was akin to raping the master's wife. However, Eve justified her relationship with the servant by bringing Adam into it. Thus, through their oneness, they completely abandoned God, the eternal Father.
If you were God, what would you do in such a position? Think about it. If you could forgive that, we could determine what kind of being God is. God is not someone who can just let anything go. Because God is absolute, that absolute is not in a bad sense, in a shameful sense, or in a sinful sense. It is in a good sense.
When anyone evaluates, they must stand on a conclusion of good meaning, saying, 'This is how it is.' God must be in a position where, whether viewed in terms of order or quality, nothing is out of place. However, that has not happened.
This is the kind of being that has become, and this is the kind of archangel that has become, and all things have been created for such a being, so what should God do? God cannot cut everything off. Originally, who is the master of these beings? It is God. Therefore, it is like sin being committed in a household centered around its master. In that case, God stands in a position of shame. God cannot help but stand in a shameful position and cannot help but feel pain from a sinful position.
When you or your mother or your siblings do something wrong in your home, does the father of that family take pride in it? If he is a thoughtful person, would he prefer that his son becomes a robber or that the family is caught up in a shameful love issue? What do you think? Which sin would be better? Among the sins related to love, which one would be worse, rape or murder? If you were the master, would you rather have it this way or that way? Of course, both are bad, but if you had to see one as worse, which would you see as worse? The issue of love is worse, right? "Yes." That's correct.
From that position, how much pain would God, who has such a son and such a servant, feel? Think about it as if you were God. How miserable would it be? From that perspective, we can conclude that God is a sorrowful God.
Next, we need to feel and understand God's position as a sinful being. We need to know the God who feels pain. Just as when a son or daughter sins and feels shame, it is not only the children who feel shame, but the parents feel even more shame than they do. God is the same.
Humans in a Position That Cannot Be Forgiven
Here in America, perhaps people do not see issues of gender as problematic these days, but from an Eastern perspective, it is unforgivable. Also, from the perspective of the Bible, this is an unforgivable fact.
So from that perspective, where does the motivation for God becoming such a being lie? Ultimately, it lies with the archangel, the servant, and humanity. If those sons and daughters or the servant realize they have sinned and go further to say, 'I deserve to die a thousand times, and how can I face my parents to ask for forgiveness? I should have disappeared, perished, and died,' then God can still have compassion. However, until now, Satan has been accusing, and humans have continued to betray God.
In the matter of individual sins, individuals can resolve them, but in the matter of love relationships, there is inevitably a triangular relationship. For example, if there is someone in the world who has forgiven the person who killed their son, they can be seen as a truly good person, but if someone forgives the person who took away their wife, they would be seen as insane. What do people in America think? They would rather die themselves.
God and Satan are in such a relationship.
If Satan hated Eve and killed her, then God could create Eve again. However, because of the entanglement of love... Love is best when it is first. The first is pure and supreme. But if the first has become like this, it cannot be recreated. If sin was committed through love, then all sons and daughters enter into a position where they cannot be forgiven.
From this perspective, we humans have become entangled. We have become one, tangled in the shame of sin. If you were to ask God, 'God, how much shame did You feel after Adam and Eve fell? How much guilt did You feel?' then God would have no choice but to be in a position where He cannot speak. It would be difficult for you to answer as well. If someone were to ask such a question, would not God be someone who could only shed tears? Would He not be a sorrowful God who cannot make excuses or ask for forgiveness?
It is we humans who have made God this way. Should such people live well or poorly? How well should they live? If that God is our Father, we should think that it would be good to do anything to comfort Him. However, even if we cry and plead for forgiveness, even if we die a hundred times, is there a way to correct it? There is no way to correct it. Those sons and daughters have become that way from the position of God's direct descendants. They have become so from a place of no sin.
So do we live in a position of no sin today? "No." If Adam and Eve could die hundreds of times to find a way to be forgiven, how many times should we die if we could do that? Should we choose the path of dying hundreds, thousands, or tens of thousands of times to be forgiven?
The Freedom That Fallen Humans Are Crying Out For Is Satan's Drug
Everyone, nowadays in America, there is a strong ideology that says, 'This is democracy, and everyone is the same, so where is the shame, and where is the guilt of conscience?' Have you thought about your shame? Have you thought about it? Have you ever had a sense of sinful consciousness?
If you were the child of a traitor, how would you feel? Would you be proud to be the child of a traitor? And if you were the child of a robber, how would you feel? Would you be proud? Next, if you had an unspeakable, beastly, shameful love relationship, would you be proud? "No." If you committed such a sin, if you were the child of someone who committed such a sin, and if you thought of yourself as their descendant, could you raise your head and say, 'Ah, I need freedom'? Could you say, 'I must just stay here as I am'? It is only natural that you cannot say that.
Before everyone can be dignified and free, what must they do first? They must die and come back to life. They must either be forgiven or turned upside down; there must be a cleansing issue. Shouldn't it be that way? Even looking at the laws of our world, it should be that way.
What happened to Adam, Eve, and the archangel? They are historical traitors. They are historical murderers. They are also representatives of historical adulterous love relationships. Their ancestor is Satan. Adam and Eve became entangled with him, becoming accomplices. Our ancestors are accomplices. You are the descendants of such ancestors.
Are you closer to yourself or to God? Are you closer to your family or to God? "I am closer to God." While you may say you are close, in reality, that is not true. You are not close. It is just a thought and words. How close have you felt to God's love? When you go abroad, you feel more of a sense of kinship than you do with God, right? Most people have not felt even that sense of kinship. Ultimately, it means you are far from God. Because God is farther from you than yourself, everything is far away.
Then, since we are far from God, who are we close to? Naturally, we are close to Satan. Since the people of this world are far from God, they must be close to Satan. Humans are born from Satan. Do people prefer principled love or illicit love? Do they prefer to uphold principled laws, or do they wish that laws would not be upheld?
When they talk about democracy and the free democratic world and say, 'Give me freedom,' are they saying, 'I will engage in principled love. I will walk the path of principled truth. I will love my country in principle'? Or are they saying, 'I will do as I please. What is principle? I will do as I wish... Love as I wish... What is law? It is whatever I want.' Which is it?
The hippies in America, most young people, the smart young people in universities, all claim to be liberal and romantic, but what are they ultimately? They are rags of illicit love, and in terms of values regarding love, they are worthless. They shake the laws that have been built up until now all at once and shake humanity all at once. Is that freedom? Do we need such freedom? Is it progress or ruin that comes from that freedom? Is it progress or ruin? "Ruin comes."
Then what is the freedom that has been mentioned, the freedom that humans are seeking? We need to understand this. It is a trap for ruin and destruction. Fundamentally, we are shameful beings among shameful beings, and we are engaging in shameful play that cannot be tolerated again. When we see this, God would not like it the most; He would hate it the most. Then who would like it? The enemy would like it the most. That is why I have new...
I would like to conclude by saying, "This freedom is the drug of Satan." What do you think of what I said? Do you think that’s true? "Yes." If there is a way to be forgiven, there is nothing we cannot do. Then, does God want to destroy this, throw it away, and leave it alone? "He wants to seek." So what should we do? Should we tell the ones He likes to just go that way, or should we pull them up in the opposite direction? "We should pull them up in the opposite direction." It means we need to pull them up in the opposite direction. If they are not coming, would it be better for God to pull them or to leave them alone? "It is better to pull them." The more we love, the more we should pull, right? Should we leave them alone? "We should pull them." Even if we pull and one arm comes out, should we hold on and keep pulling, or should we let go because it cannot come out? "Even if it comes out...." 

The Bible says if your eye causes you to sin, pluck it out, and if your hand causes you to sin, cut it off. God has said such things. Now, have you thought about how serious God's position is regarding sin? You might think, "Well, if the eye sins just once, we can just leave it alone and forgive it, why should we pluck it out?" But when we desire perfection, we cannot do otherwise. 

When God tries to pull you, are you the one who cries and makes a fuss, or are you the one who says, "I will go quickly," and goes willingly? What kind of person are you? Are you the one who goes reluctantly, crying, or are you the one who goes joyfully? Which one are you among the three? "I go joyfully." You shed tears saying you won’t go, you are dragged along reluctantly, and you go joyfully saying, "Ah, this is where I need to go." Which one is it among these three? "Ah, then I must go. I can't go without a command." Is that it? 

Then how was it before you entered the Unification Church? How was it before you entered the Unification Church? Did you cry? You neither cried nor followed along unwillingly, so you were foolish and paralyzed. Such a person cannot even be considered a person, right? You didn’t know how to cry and couldn’t follow along unwillingly, so you were paralyzed, paralyzed. 

Should such a person be treated as a person or not? That is who we were. When we, such people, came to believe in the Unification Church and said, "I must go even if I have to crawl," how revolutionary is that? Is it just a little bit? Is it just this much? (Expressing with action) This is a revolution that has never happened in history, and it is greater than the world turning. You did not realize that such an event occurred within yourselves. You have not clearly recognized it until now. Even after coming here, you still do not know it. Now, you must clearly understand this. Our attitude should be to stand with such pride and autonomy.

Now, if I give you a doctorate, make you successful, and make you a senator in the U.S., would you go if I told you to throw this away? "No." Hearing your answer, it’s a "no," right? You must have such pride. You must stand firm saying, "I cannot trade my dignity for the authority of any king in the world or any president." Moreover, you should have the confidence that "not only in this era but also no past hero, not even Jesus, Confucius, or Buddha can compare to me. I will overcome history." And you should think, "If there is a way to remove the historical shame and correct the historical sins, I want to try that." Only then can you be seen as someone qualified to enter such a position.

Now, when we ask if there is a way to correct this shame and sin, how wonderful it would be if there is one, and how miserable it would be if there isn’t. Now, you have come to know God. Before such a God, we have recognized the shame of our ancestors, and we have understood that our ancestors lived shamefully through history, and today we have realized that the world we live in is shameful. What can we boast about before God, having left this? Can we boast about ourselves? We cannot be that way. We are descendants who have made ourselves shameful and have been subjected to sinful humiliation, and we know that we do not have the qualifications to stand before God. If He forgives such a person and if there is something He can like and require, if there is a way for Him to rejoice and forget His shame and escape from sin, can I not do anything? "Yes."

To relieve God's resentment, there is no choice but to walk the path of death. So what should we do? Even if God kills me a thousand or ten thousand times, if it can relieve His heart to kill and resurrect me, to make me suffer more, to kill me again and resurrect me to suffer even more miserably, if it can be repeated millions of times for God's heart to be relieved, then I have no choice but to choose that path. Whether it is three times, a hundred times, a thousand times, or ten thousand times, if I can do it, I must have the mindset to choose that path. There is no other way. That is the only way.

By doing so, God should be able to say, "Oh, this guy! That’s how it should be." If I continue to do such things, God will say, "Okay, let’s stop now." At that time, I should be able to say, "No, someone like me needs to die more. I need to suffer more. To relieve Your resentment, I must be more miserable." 

If I can do that, God will say, "Okay, I need to stop now. I have lost to you. Because of you, I will forgive everything, forget everything." There will be a turning point where He can say, "I will resolve the issues that Adam and Eve caused." You need to go until that point. There is something there; that is the boundary line. You must think about crossing that boundary line where God and I may diverge. 

When you cross over, do you want to leave even a little behind, or do you want to cross over completely so that God can say, "Oh, that’s good!"? "God said it was good...." Then, when God kills me and resurrects me, should I think, "Ah, I have now paid my indemnity, so since I died and was resurrected, I should enter heaven"? Should I think that way or not? "I should not think that way." 

Now you know this. Therefore, because the fallen Adam and Eve made God cry and made Him sad and suffer, we who need to restore must find the path of death to make God happy and make Him dance. 

Look. God's tears are with God Himself, with His sons and daughters, and they reach down to the descendants. God's sad tears, you see. The history of tears falls down. Because humans have caused sadness to God, God's tears and sorrowful position gradually fall down. 

When Adam and Eve fell, did God shed tears or not? "He shed tears." How many tears do you think He shed? The more you think about it, the more it is astonishing, and the more you think about it, the sadder it becomes.... What do you think it was like? The more you think about it, does the sadness fade away, or does it come back to life? "It would have come back to life." When descendants keep going down the path of sin and committing sins, it would have been like stabbing God in the heart. 

So, when we talk about the sad history, who has the longest history, and who has suffered the most? If someone has suffered, who has suffered the most? It is God. It is undoubtedly God. Because of us, because of humanity, because of me, who will take responsibility to resolve that? To make such a God happy, as I said earlier, "I will stand in a position where I can endure a sorrow and misery beyond what You have suffered." 

You must become a responsible person who can educate, saying, "Adam, why did you do that? It could have been this way." You must educate Noah, saying, "Noah, why did you do that? It could have been this way." You must educate Abraham, saying, "Abraham, why did you offer that sacrifice?" You must educate Moses, saying, "Moses, why did you break the tablets?" You must educate Jesus, saying, "Jesus, why did you do that?" You must find yourself responsible for reaching a position beyond them. At that time, you must feel the sorrow of your ancestors who failed and were sad, hundreds of times over, and you must realize that without connecting this process of struggling to correct it, there is no way to relieve God's historical sorrow. 

Now, if you face a difficult situation, do you have the confidence to pray, "God, help me. Oh, I am sad, so God, please help me"? You must realize that you cannot pray. We humans must first recognize how much greater God's desire and request for us has been than our prayers for Him. You must know that God has been praying for us more than any person in history has prayed to Him. He has been praying for the sons and daughters who can relieve that sorrow I mentioned earlier. That has been continuing from the day of the fall until now. 

But do you ask for blessings? Do you expect to receive blessings? Will the one who says, "God, make me suffer and put me in a place of death to relieve Your resentment" receive blessings? "The one in a difficult situation." Now you understand. You must discover the joy that comes from the fact that by walking the path of suffering, the sorrow of heaven and earth is being relieved. When there is suffering, we must comfort God and pray, "How much have You suffered in such a position? My wish is to restore a heart that can make You happy through me." That is our responsibility. Do you understand? "Yes." 

Now that you know this, you must feel that your breath and life are for the purpose of relieving God's sorrow. You must also think that all your feelings of sorrow and pain are for the purpose of relieving God's sorrow. This must flow as the main current. Whether I sing, express, write, or speak, all of this is to contribute to this.... I must have the conviction that I will live and go for this purpose. 

We have historically failed, and we are different from our ancestors who were decadent. Therefore, we must determine that this path is our path. "By finding you, I have found the world, by finding you, I have lost sorrow and pain, by finding you, liberation has occurred, by you joy and love have come, by you families and nations have been established, and by you a joyful world could arise." Isn’t that what God would hope for? 

In other words, you must become someone who can hear from God, "I want to talk to you, I want to communicate with you, I want to give you my things, and I want to receive your things." Thus, if through me God can be liberated from suffering, sorrow, and pain, and can march toward a kingdom of glory, joy, and freedom, where both can rejoice together and find families together, and cooperate to find nations and the world, then what more could we hope for? What more could God hope for from humanity? There is nothing beyond that. 

Therefore, the first issue is not to liberate the world. It is to liberate God. Then, we will liberate the families that God desires, and then...
isn't it?’라는 생각이 들 수 있다는 거예요. 그러니까 여러분들이 지금부터라도 그럴 수 없다는 것을 느끼고, 지금부터라도 여러분이 나가서 무엇인가를 해야 한다는 것을 느껴야 되는 거예요. 

여러분이 지금 이 자리에 있는 것은 단순히 개인적인 이유가 아니라, 하나님과 인류를 위해서 존재하는 것입니다. 여러분이 스스로를 위해서가 아니라, 여러분의 후손과 인류를 위해서 무엇인가를 해야 한다는 것을 느껴야 합니다. 여러분이 지금 이 자리에 있는 것은 그 책임을 다하기 위해서입니다. 

이제 여러분은 하나님이 원하시는 나라를 해방시키고, 세상을 해방시키기 위해서 나아가야 합니다. 하나님이 부끄러움을 풀 수 있는 길은 이것밖에 없다는 것을 확실히 깨달아야 합니다. 여러분은 영광의 자식이 되기를 원하나요? 그렇다면 여러분은 부끄러운 길이 아닌 영광의 길을 선택해야 합니다. 

이제 여러분은 책임이 있습니다. 여러분은 선생님이 자신을 위해서 무엇을 해주길 바라는 것이 아니라, 후손을 위해서 도와달라고 요청해야 합니다. 여러분이 지금 이 자리에 있는 것은 단순히 개인적인 이유가 아니라, 하나님과 인류를 위해서 존재하는 것입니다. 

하나님을 해방하고, 세상을 해방한 후에야 여러분이 해방된다는 것을 잊지 말아야 합니다. 여러분은 이제부터 하나님의 수치를 감소시킬 수 있다는 여기에 집중해야 합니다. 모든 면에서 최고가 되어 수치스러운 인간에서 해방받아야 합니다. 

여러분이 원리를 배울 때, 그것은 남의 것이 아닙니다. 여러분은 아담이 되고, 노아가 되고, 아브라함이 되어야 합니다. 여러분이 이러한 실체적인 부활체로서 실패했기 때문에, 하나님의 슬픔을 느끼면서 강의를 들어야 합니다. 

여러분은 이제부터 하나님과 인류를 위해서 무엇인가를 해야 합니다. 여러분이 지금 이 자리에 있는 것은 그 책임을 다하기 위해서입니다. 여러분은 하나님을 위해서, 인류를 위해서 무엇인가를 해야 합니다. 

이제 여러분은 하나님이 원하시는 나라를 해방시키고, 세상을 해방시키기 위해서 나아가야 합니다. 여러분은 영광의 자식이 되기를 원하나요? 그렇다면 여러분은 부끄러운 길이 아닌 영광의 길을 선택해야 합니다.
has been the center of their lives. Their lives were not centered around themselves but were initiated by God. The fame they achieved and the status they hold today are not merely the results of their own efforts. This too was guided by God's direction and in accordance with God's command.

In our faith life, the most pressing issue is how we relate to all the vague spiritual targets and how we establish a connection with them. A fundamental condition for this is the principle. The relationships formed in our faith life are where the issues arise. Next, material aspects become a concern. Then, knowledge and understanding come into play. People inevitably make judgments and decisions through their understanding, so how we connect the results of our understanding to real problems is what matters.

However, it is difficult to find such motivations centered on actual people as targets in our faith life. Therefore, we cannot help but set the historical figures from Adam to the present as standards for how faith leaders have fought to maintain their faith. How those central figures dealt with interpersonal relationships, material relationships, or all social environments must be our standard.

When we look at figures like Noah, Abraham, Moses, and John the Baptist, we become curious about the motivations that led them to fulfill their historical missions. Their lives were not centered around personal ambitions but were initiated with God at the center. They did not start from themselves but from God. Their fame and the status they have achieved today are not merely the results of their own efforts. This too was guided by God's direction and in accordance with God's command.
Because they stood in the place of the substitute, we know that they have become the objects of our reverence.

38 Faith and Reality  
How have the figures of the providence resolved all their problems?  
We need to understand what path they have walked in the course of their lives. It is natural that they faced real-life issues in their daily lives, and we discover here that they always had conflicting realities. When confronted with such problems, we learn that they did not act according to their own will.  
At such times, we know that they were representatives who made efforts to establish heaven and follow the path determined by heaven. Furthermore, because they were such responsible figures, we understand that as the providence of their time changed, the environment they faced also changed, leading to increasing persecution and difficulties.  
First, the position they took was not one that was always welcomed; it was a position of persecution. Therefore, we can find that they lived a lonely life.  
Because they could not engage in personal interactions, they had no choice but to express their desire to speak about God, rather than having the environment to do so. Moreover, when they faced external issues such as material problems or difficulties, the means to resolve them as humans were limited. Thus, they were in a position where they could not help but desire to discuss and resolve these issues with heaven, hoping that heaven would motivate and provide solutions. After that, they found themselves in a position where all the issues regarding their necessary understanding and practical matters were narrow and blocked. Consequently, they had to discuss all these problems with heaven, hoping that they would be recognized and resolved through heaven. We discover here that this environment allowed them to make efforts to unify everything with God.  
Humans need a practical counterpart. However, because they have been rejected by all practical counterparts, they approach heaven with a more earnest heart than seeking a practical counterpart. They want to live centered around their actual lives, and they find themselves in a position where they cannot help but live in relation to heaven.  
As real-life problems become increasingly narrow, they hope to transcend their loneliness by centering on heaven and to encompass real-life issues from a position that opposes reality, feeling joy and determining how to establish their central values. It is a problem that should not lead to despair or disappointment just because it is narrowing. Despair and disappointment must absolutely be avoided. Complaining should not be an option.  
When God created this universe, He did so with a posture of joy and satisfaction. Therefore, the question becomes how to maintain peace, gratitude, and joy in one’s heart even when faced with persecution or narrow peaks. This determines whether one can be in a position to relate to God. From such a point, heaven can begin to establish a relationship with us.  
You are likely familiar with Francesco (Giovanni Francesco Bernardone), a representative who lived a life of poverty during the Middle Ages. He advocated for poverty. Even when faced with difficult living conditions and external environments, he did not complain, feel sorrow, or suffer. If he had felt that way, he could not have inherited heaven’s will. However, because he stood in a position of gratitude, hope, and seeking something new amidst suffering, God cooperated with him. Thus, we can find a new era there.  
We must always realize that we stand at the intersection of two worlds. He was in a position where he could complain as much as he wanted. Do you have the qualifications to be a counterpart before God, the subject?  
When you begin your faith life, it is easy to think, “I call upon God and believe in Him, but He does not establish a direct relationship with me or help me.” However, if God only helps you in your current position, you must consider what value such a God has. If you are in a position where you have a relationship with God, that may be true, but such a relationship has not yet been established. When you, as individuals practicing your faith, consider whether you have the qualifications to be an object before God, the subject, you may wonder if you truly do. God, once He decides something, does not change and cannot help but act according to that decision for thousands or millions of years. However, when you look at your hearts, they change several times a day. If you have made a resolution now, how long can you carry that resolution? God can hold onto a decision for thousands of years and keep it forever. He does not waver. You might say, “I am going for the purpose,” but will you continue that way until the end of this year, or the year after, or for 10, 20 years, or your whole life? This is something that can easily be let go. And when it comes to going forward, it often depends on whether you feel good about it; if you feel bad, you might say you cannot go.

When these two collide, the changing will break away, but the unchanging will remain intact. It is a clash between death and life. At that moment, we must overcome death and remain in life. It is a given that only by overcoming such a process can one relate to God.

5)
Today and Tomorrow
We feel that days are passing by without our attention. We know that this day called today exists to carry on to tomorrow. At this time, I would like to speak on the topic of ‘Today and Tomorrow.’
We must align ourselves with the direction that God is guiding today and tomorrow. When we welcome spring and see flowers blooming and new leaves sprouting in nature, we come to realize that this spring must come after winter. We also know that after this spring, summer will come. Therefore, we understand that today, this spring, is a day of preparation to inherit summer.
We can think this way when observing the seasons, but we can also think this way when looking at people. When we look at a young man, we feel something like spring in him. We know that after the youth period, the middle age period will come. We also understand that he will go through old age while walking the path of life. In one era, when we look at a person’s entire life, we realize that if there is this current era, there will be a next era.
When we look at the current world situation, we find ourselves in a complex situation, and we wonder what kind of era will come after this present age.
We think the same about the human world, but we also think the same about God’s providential restoration. We cannot help but consider that there is a current age and a next age in God’s providential restoration.
Then, how do the today of humanity and the today of God’s providential restoration differ? This is a question that we naturally cannot avoid thinking about. We cannot help but consider how the future after God’s providential restoration will differ from the future we desire.
Human beings are not always aligned with the direction in which God is walking and guiding, so we cannot see ourselves as aligned with the direction of God’s providential restoration today and tomorrow. Therefore, religion always raises and addresses the issue of the relationship between God and humanity.
The question of whether God is coming down or going up, and understanding how God’s providence is in the present, is undoubtedly the most precious issue. If God is going up, we should not go down. If God is coming down, we should not go up. If God is going left, we should not go right. There is a problem here that requires us to always walk in the same direction. We must always be aware of whether God is going with a joyful heart or a sorrowful heart.
No matter how difficult it may be, no matter how downward the path may seem, if tomorrow is guaranteed and the foundation of hope resides there, we cannot help but go down. No matter how good the upward path may be, if tomorrow is not guaranteed there, we cannot help but retreat from it. This is the same for God’s providence and our human lives.

The Human Who Could Not Welcome the Today of Completion and the Direction of Restoration
Today and tomorrow can also be thought of as a boundary line. When looking from one country to another, when the country on this side becomes strong, it can absorb the country on the other side. From this perspective, this moment I am in today is undoubtedly the present.
If we trace back this time to the very beginning, to God’s position at creation, there must have been a today for God at the time of creation. That time of creation cannot be seen as anything other than a preparation period for realizing the ideal world. God completed creation. After that, Adam and Eve entered the process of growth. This process can be seen as the practical age. The purpose of going through such a period is to see the today of completion, which was God’s plan and the ideal of creation.
Then, did humanity welcome the today of completion? No, they did not. Did they welcome the day when they could practice according to God’s will? No, they did not. We come to realize that while the preparation standard has been completed, the practical standard has not yet been surpassed, which is the current state of God’s providence and God’s position.
What is the standard of hope that we desire? It is to complete through the process of practice according to God’s will. That is the standard we hope for. We know that God’s work is still incomplete. It is an undeniable fact that there is a path we must walk and a path we must fulfill.
The fact that humanity has fallen is a miserable truth for us. The fact that there was a day of the fall, that there was such a today, is something we must recognize as negating the whole. No matter how much a fallen person practices, it cannot align with the practical standard that God desires or the standard of completion that God seeks. No matter how well God has prepared, we must understand that it cannot just remain as it is.
The day of the fall was the moment that negated even what God had prepared. Therefore, when we look at the human-centered restoration providence today, we must not just leave the completion standards of preparation and practice as they are, but we must prepare in new areas, practice in new areas, and seek completion in new areas. This is the position of God that we must recognize.
We must not remain in the place prepared by God but leave that place and seek a new path. This is the direction and position we are in. Therefore, humanity cannot move to a position where they can hope for more based on the standard of conscience, but must engage in a play of retreat even from the standard of conscience.
The fact that humanity has fallen can also serve as a dramatic element that can evoke the sorrow of what was prepared. It can become a motive that recalls sorrow. It is not an easy task to place a fallen person, who brings sorrow, back into the standard of that generation and position that was prepared without sorrow. Even if we, fallen people, have completed restoration, reaching the original standard that must be achieved without falling is nearly impossible.
In friendships, we see that among the closest friends, one friend can become an extreme enemy. When that friend who has hurt us comes back and says they want to return to the old friendship, can we just accept them as they are? When we think about this, we recall that we, as humans before God, are in the same position.
To what extent have humans brought mistakes before God? They have made a tremendous mistake that has turned the achievement of creation upside down and made human history so miserable. This is not just a problem confined to themselves; the results of this mistake have manifested before God. In other words, they have become a threat to the issue of life and a threat to the issue of love. The fact that God, the subject of life and love, can be threatened by this is something we cannot forget.
How should fallen humanity approach God, who is sorrowful?
For such humans to achieve restoration and completion, how do they overcome the heart of the wounds inflicted upon God? How do they discard that feeling? How do they move to a place where they do not feel such emotions? This is undoubtedly a very difficult issue. Even if they prepare anew with such a sorrowful heart, can they reach the standards that God has prepared if they only hold onto ideals? They cannot. We realize here that this is an important issue in God’s providential restoration. We must reflect on whether we are in a position to say to God, ‘I will prepare anew for you.’
If we stand in a place of sorrowful God and think about ourselves, ‘Who am I?’ and take a step forward from where we stand, it is an undeniable fact that God remains in a place where He cannot help but feel sorrow. If God has not resolved His sorrow, then I cannot claim to have resolved mine either. If God cannot be joyful about me, then I cannot claim to be joyful about God. There should be no sorrow in God; there should only be joy. Before human hope, there must be God’s hope.
Today, before we humans take pride in ourselves, there must be a place where God can take pride. From this perspective, what should be the attitude of a fallen descendant who wishes to follow the will of God’s restoration providence and hopes to enter a new place of completion within that providence? Considering all of this, it is undoubtedly true that one should not establish oneself.
Humans must repent with the entire lineage of parents and ancestors mobilized.
When we think that God has first experienced sorrow, suffering, and is in a miserable position, we must consider what attitude we should have to allow God to be joyful, to have hope, to practice goodness, and to want to prepare anew.
What is the only path for humanity to return to heaven? There is undoubtedly a need for the word repentance. That is why John the Baptist and Jesus came to this earth and said, ‘Repent, for the kingdom of heaven is at hand.’ What does repentance mean? It means settlement.
So how should we repent? Can I just repent alone? Can it be done just by my repentance? It cannot. The reason I stand in this sorrowful position today is that this sorrow has continued through thousands of generations of ancestors. Therefore, in repentance, we must stand in a place where the entire lineage of parents and ancestors is mobilized to repent.
Among those present, there may be someone who thinks, ‘What sin do I have? I may have been born this way, but I have no conscience to feel guilty.’ But that is not true. While you sit here calmly, your appearance is not just your own. You bear a little bit of the appearance of each of your ancestors. It is as if you possess parts of thousands of generations of ancestors.
In God’s eyes, there may be elements of sin committed by your ancestors visible within you. Would God want to take an interest in you while looking at such things? It cannot be. Can God, who must stand on a principled position, govern this realm of non-principle that resulted from the fall? God cannot directly handle this. God created people in principle at the time of creation. Just as He mobilized angels for cooperation, He can only do so with angels.
When angels are commanded to work, if they come to know that the humans on earth are the descendants of fallen humans, will they praise them? Has there been anyone in this world who has received praise from angels? No. Then, what kind of person can angels sympathize with and come to visit? It is someone who does not elevate themselves but feels inadequate and feels shame before heaven and earth, someone who thinks there is no sinner like themselves. Only such a person can create a path for angels to come.
When thinking about this restoration, we must consider where restoration begins. If we acknowledge our current fallen selves, the term restoration corresponds to tomorrow. It is not about simply adapting the current position to connect to tomorrow; it is about completely settling the current position.
To cross the boundary of tomorrow through today, there must be a revolution, a collapse, a reform. Such actions must occur within myself. It is a matter of experiencing both collapse and hope. Collapse must be settled with today, and hope must be fulfilled with tomorrow.
What kind of place is such a place? It is a place that, no matter how much one searches, can only be a place of sacrifice. To sacrifice, one must reach a level of self-awareness that says, ‘I am the greatest sinner in history.’ One must realize, ‘I am a sinner who should receive punishment that has never existed in history. I must receive judgment that has never existed in history.’

No matter how painful, no matter how despised, no matter what treatment one receives, one must have a heart that can be grateful. Even if one enters a place of ruin, one should not seek sympathy by saying, ‘God, I am ruined,’ but rather should have the heart that says, ‘I do not mind being ruined, but I hope you can be liberated and joyful.’ We must recognize that this heart becomes the new condition of sacrifice.
When considering the thousands of generations of ancestors, God will think of the wrongs committed by the ancestors. Therefore, ‘In any era, your ancestors have made mistakes that...

God is the judge of the universe, Jesus is the lawyer, and Satan is the prosecutor.
Have you ever thought about the hearts of those who stand in court or at trial? The prosecutor tries to charge them with whatever crime they can and wants to put them away. If there is even a little sin, they will try to beat them down. If there is even a small mistake, they will try to bind them. But have we committed even a small sin before God? How big is it? How big is it? It has made it possible for millions to be sacrificed and has put all of history in a position where it could perish. The sin that has encroached upon God is vast. It is because of our sins that God has been unable to act as God.

So, who can forgive that sin? Who can forgive it? Is it enough for a judge or a father to say they forgive? No. Only God can forgive, and there is no other way.

We, such people, stand in court, but while the prosecutor may charge even a small sin, there is a lawyer there. The lawyer is the one who argues that it is not a sin. The lawyer dislikes the idea of having committed a sin and prefers to say it has not been committed. Who do you prefer among them?

Then, will the judge listen to the lawyer’s words and make a judgment, or will he listen to the prosecutor’s words and make a judgment? How does the judge make a judgment? The judge will make a judgment based on the motivation behind the sin. Isn’t that so? If the motivation is for the sake of others, it can be forgiven; if the motivation is for one’s own desires, a heavier punishment will be given.

So, God is the judge of the universe. What is Jesus? He is the lawyer, and what is Satan? He is the prosecutor. Satan takes you and drags you before the judge, saying, ‘This person has sinned, so he must be sent to hell immediately.’ But Jesus says, ‘God, I have shed blood for You and worked for You, so these people must be sent to heaven, not hell. They must be sent according to my wishes.’ Jesus argues like this. Then how must God make a judgment? The same way. He must judge based on the motivation.

Adam sinned for himself, but the person who has come here has not sinned for himself and has not been dragged here for himself, but has the motivation that he was dragged here while sacrificing for others. If he can have that motivation, there may be a way to escape punishment. This is a natural statement. If one has such motivation, they would not even be dragged to court, but even if they are, they will surely find a way to be released immediately. In this sense, the principle that one must prioritize others before oneself is undoubtedly an absolute principle in religious life.

The more one repeats the same thing, the more they become an expert
When you study now, those who know nothing only think of the principle, but those who know must plan to conquer theologians, doctors of theology, and anyone else. Therefore, do not think about evangelizing those who are less capable than you. Evangelize those who are more capable than you.

Training ends here. "Ah, I have heard the principle a few times and understand it, so I wish to stop now." There are many such statements. You will understand when you study, but when you hear the principle once, you think of it as a fist. After hearing it once, you think, "Ah, the principle is like this." However, "The principle is flat. It is flat and half. But upon closer inspection, it is not so." It changes. It goes deeper inside.

Then, it is not just this; you realize that there is also a counterpart. You understand that this does not remain still but competes with each other, and you also understand the cycles. The teacher knows the principle but still enjoys listening to the principle. There is no end to it.

The taste of rice does not come from biting into it once; it becomes tastier the more you bite into it. Those who do it once cannot become experts. The more one does the same thing ten times, a hundred times, a thousand times, the more they become an expert.

There are many principles in physics or Archimedes' principles, but the people who discovered those principles did not just read them once and find them. They thought about them repeatedly, hundreds, thousands of times, and then understood the principles.

The same goes for learning a language. When learning a foreign language, can you just do it once a day? You must memorize and memorize and memorize until it becomes a formula.

By polishing like that, you create a foundation. You must create your own foundation. You must set it up correctly. It must not be wrong.

If you want to become a world-renowned lecturer, you must listen to all the words of the leaders of the Unification Church scattered around the world. Therefore, even when studying, it is different from yesterday. It is different from yesterday. It is the preparation for tomorrow, deeper preparation, higher preparation... When watching a movie, the quality is different between someone who watches the same thing ten times and someone who watches it once. **Brothers and Me**

We know that before the existence of "brothers and me," there are parents who gave birth to me. Those parents also have siblings and parents. If we trace our ancestors back, we eventually reach Adam and Eve, the progenitors of humanity.

One cannot become a mature person without experiencing the love of children. When we reach Adam and Eve, who are their parents? They are none other than God. If God is the parent, then Adam and Eve, as children, must become one with that parent.

The love between parents and children comes from the parents, which means the love of the father and mother. From the moment we are born, we receive the love of our parents. And as long as our parents are alive, we receive love in our boyhood, youth, and adulthood, regardless of the stage. As we grow up receiving this parental love, the horizontal love of spouses naturally develops for each individual. For the love of spouses to continue, they must have children and love those children.

From this perspective, the progenitors of humanity grow up receiving God's love and become spouses, and in love, everyone is composed of pairs. In this view, both those who receive parental love and those who give it are all brothers.

Parents cannot know what love is without their own children. True love can only be felt when there is an object. Siblings grow up without knowing what parental love is, but when they grow up, marry, and have children, they come to understand parental love. In other words, one must start from being a parent, go around, and return to being a parent to understand.

So, where should we set the standard for a complete and perfected person? While parents may be seen as mature, if those parents are not mature both horizontally and vertically, they cannot be considered complete individuals. When Adam and Eve mature by receiving God's love and become one centered on God, they enter a place where they can unite in a relationship of mutuality, and there the love that God intended to realize through completion is fulfilled.

Love is learned from parents. 

When Adam and Eve become one centered on God, a form is established. However, to achieve a flat form, they must have children. This creates a horizontal relationship. However, one must understand that a vertical relationship cannot be formed without this.

The love of spouses is one, while parental love is more than two in a vertical relationship. The question then becomes which is more important. The love of spouses has a relative relationship, but because it is one, the vertical aspect must be central.

A vertical relationship extends the love between parents and children. Parents, spouses, and children become the principle of vertical relationships. When they completely unite, they form a family. When the love of spouses expands, it connects to parental love. When parents become parents through the relationship of spouses, the children must also have the same size and length of parental love. Then, how should the love between siblings be? By what standard should they love? They should love each other as the father loves the son.

Who do we learn love from? We must learn it from our parents. The reason for breakdowns in families is that love is severed. Therefore, to continue love, we must step on the love of spouses centered on parents and prepare to inherit that love from both parents and spouses.

Preparation to inherit love must be done through siblings. If there are siblings, one must love that younger sibling as one loves their own mother. A female sibling must love her older brother as she loves her father. Male and female siblings must feel the love of parents and children for each other. In other words, just as a father loves his son, an older brother must love his younger brother, and just as a mother loves her daughter, an older sister must love her younger sister.

What if there are no siblings? That is like having no object. Because of siblings, we can realize a substantial existence that cares for one another. Siblings come from the bodies of the father and mother, so they represent the parents. Each of us is like a combination of half of the father and half of the mother, and what must bind this together? It must be bound by love.

In order to be completely restored, Abel must lead Cain with love.

The most important thing in restoration is Cain and Abel. Therefore, we must understand what Cain and Abel are. Cain and Abel are representatives of the parents and bodies bound by parental love. Just as spouses love each other, if siblings love each other, they become completely one.

Abel must restore Cain, but where is that ideal position? It is a position that replaces the parents, a position that guides with love. Abel must stand in the position that replaces the parents. Otherwise, he cannot lead Cain to the ideal position of restoration. If he places him there without passing through that love, he will not feel happiness.

Since the love of the human world began with the love of parents and spouses, there can be no other love. If children stand in the same position to inherit the tradition of love that their parents had, it becomes ideal. If children can engage in the love of parents and spouses, ideal love is determined.

Abel dreams and wishes for the restoration of ideal love, so he must engage in the love of spouses and parents. Cain was born but is in the realm of fall, so he is like one who has not been born. Abel must emulate God's love. And while God loves Abel as a child, because it is relative, Abel must also love Cain in a way that is reciprocal. Only then will he follow.

So how should one love from the position of a parent? If I have not experienced parental love, I cannot reproduce that love. Abel must feel parental love and at the same time feel relative love. This must be centered on God, and he must strive to maintain that relative love until death. Abel must do this in loving Cain.

For the person one loves, one must take on all hardships and try to make that person comfortable. This is the same for parental love and relative love. True parents or spouses love beyond life itself. If Abel loves Cain in this way, he can be said to be completely restored.

When a complete being is given, two complete beings come together to create a complete counterpart for the subject. This is what the principle teaches.

For humans, the two most important and cherished things are life and love. When we give something complete, we feel that something complete returns. Looking at the time of Jesus, Israel stood completely in the evil position of Cain, but Jesus did not curse Cain; he sacrificed his life. This is an astonishing fact. From here, the history of return began. Abel comes to the position of God, and Cain comes to the position of Abel. Advancing to the ideal place is restoration.

True love is wanting to give and give again to the object.

The title of today’s message is "Brothers and Me," and to restore, we must have siblings. Restoration must be centered on God's love, so the love of siblings must exceed the ideal love of parents and spouses.

In the path of restoration, children must restore parents, and to restore parents, one must restore God. In other words, Cain and Abel must become one for parents to emerge, and spouses must become one for God to emerge. For God's love to reach the children, there must be a relative standard of parental love. Without such a standard, it cannot come.

Now, let us specifically explore how Cain and Abel should love each other. To love means to give one's life along with love, which is sacrifice. Sacrifice means giving something complete to receive something complete in return; this is the principle of restoration. We must always think about how to apply the principle of restoration to the issue of "me and my brother."

When there are more than three people, there must be a center that becomes the parental and object relationship. This is parental love and spousal love. If parental love and spousal love are not expressed among siblings, they cannot become a relative standard. In a group, the leader becomes the representative of the parents. Those children must love on behalf of the parents and express spousal love, and they must love one another. That is the ideal type. It becomes the ideal family type.

We must love, unite, and be able to give and sacrifice based on this principle of love. The subject of love is Abel, so the subject must give first to the object. This is the essence of love. When parents love their children, or in relationships between spouses or siblings, the person in the position of the subject must give first. Even if the children do not recognize the love that parents have for them, the natural love flows down in joy.

Heavenly families do not come about by force but are formed automatically in joy. Even in love, it must not be only about receiving; the act of giving and receiving must happen naturally for ideal love to be established. In restoring Cain and Abel, we must also make this connection of love well. True love is the object...

Triangle Relationship
Today, I will speak on the topic of "Triangle Relationship." 
Humans placed in a triangle relationship between God and Satan due to the fall. 

When you watch a movie, you sometimes see a triangle relationship formed around a man or a woman, where they are in conflict. When we watch such movies and consider who we want to win, it goes without saying that we hope the just side wins. Also, the person caught between the two would naturally wish for the honest and righteous person to win. 

The fact that we humans have fallen means that we are in a position similar to a triangle relationship. Here, people are placed in the middle, and God and Satan are currently fighting. In the human world, if you have power, everything can be resolved, but for eternal beings like spirits, power alone is not enough. 

So, what determines victory? It is a matter of principle. God and Satan are always fighting over people, and people cannot just remain passive; ultimately, the question is what they choose to take. When two sides fight in a triangle relationship, the being in the middle cannot just remain still. If they can support the good side, they should do so quickly. That way, both sides can resolve their issues faster. 

If there is an evil Satan and God, and a person is caught in between, what can that person do? The path of religious people is to reject the evil Satan and support God. However, this triangle relationship does not end in one fight. The personal struggle gradually expands, developing the conflict of this triangle relationship. 

God and Satan have been fighting for thousands of years over history to bring humans to their side, yet today, humans live without realizing they are in such a struggle. God and Satan cannot afford to relax or yield even for a moment in this fight. However, humans are not in such a serious position, which is always a problem. The fact that we are in such a triangle relationship indicates our fallen state, and if that is certain, we must recognize that we are in a very fearful position. 

If a person who was in the middle comes to God's side and cooperates to become one, what happens if they then go to the side of Satan? Satan will undoubtedly hate them even more. If one goes from God's side to Satan's side, God will also dislike them. But does Satan welcome them? Rather than saying, "Oh, you came at the right time," the unforgiving evil Satan will have no choice but to punish them. Evil Satan only punishes... 

We must learn to be grateful for God's greater forgiveness. 
People, including yourselves, are always fluctuating. Therefore, God cannot help but think about what kind of strategy He must employ to save these changeable humans. If Satan forgives humans, what happens? Then God will try to offer an even greater forgiveness than Satan. If there is a competition of forgiveness, humans cannot help but welcome the one who forgives more greatly. Ultimately, we will say that a better person has a greater heart for forgiveness. Therefore, in terms of forgiveness, Satan cannot win against God. 

When we look at humans, God is like a true father, while Satan is like a stepfather, someone who has forcibly established a relationship with us. So, when it comes to true forgiveness, who is closer? It must undoubtedly be God. Wouldn't you agree? 

Is there someone dozing off? Should we stop talking? "No." What good is it to doze off from Sunday morning? If you doze off, you are being drawn to Satan. You doze off without realizing Satan is here; if you knew, could you doze off? 

In this light, even regarding forgiveness, Satan cannot win against God. Therefore, Satan, who is opposed to God, can only say, "If you forgive, I will not forgive." Thus, we can theoretically deduce that there cannot be two worlds. 

In the world, when someone makes a mistake, a person who forgives well and forgives greatly is called a person of character and a great person. They become an object of admiration. "No." If you have been forgiven once and twice, you should feel sorry. If you are a true person, that is. If you are dazed and do not know how to be grateful, what does that mean? If He looked like a yellow person, would you say, "That's the God of yellow people; He is not my God"? "No." Therefore, color is not the issue.

In love, there is only one love; in eternal, unchanging love, that love is paramount, and color or shape does not matter. Rather, when a black person sees a white person and says, "Hey, you're my son," and the white person responds, "Oh, really? My father!" and cries, how much more lovable would that be? This is because they do not live in the same place and have shared all sorrows while traveling the country, leading to a deeper motivation for love.

Now, if there is a father who has worked hard for 6,000 years to find his son, would he approach saying, "You are black, and you are white"? (Laughter) Is color the issue? The only issue is the undeniable fact that he is a son; everything else does not matter. The son is the issue.

"God has worked hard for 6,000 years, ruining nations and the world, to finally meet me." Have you ever thought about that? Have you truly felt it? If I found the father who has searched for me like that, how joyful would I be? How happy would I be? Even if my mouth were to split from smiling, my tongue twisted, and my eyes turned upside down, that would be fine. Even if I didn't eat for hours, days, or months, I should have a heart that can rejoice, right? And if I met that father who has worked so hard, wouldn't I want to do something good for him, to make him happy, and forget all the hard work I put in for him?

As the father becomes happier, I should have the heart to do something that can make him forget all the hardships he endured, saying, "Hey, don't suffer anymore." I should want to do something that can make the father happy. "Now, Father, I am not the only son; there are many other brothers, so you shouldn't suffer so much to find them. I will take care of it, so you can stop and go there." If I say that, would it be unfilial? If I can do better than the father, "Sure!" The father would be happy.

If there is such a son, is that for himself? Would anyone want to suffer for such hardship? If there is such a son, for whom would he want to suffer? It would only be for the father and for the brothers. That is the position of a filial son. That is the position of someone who, as a fallen human being, having betrayed the father, wants to convey the grace of gratitude for meeting the father again to all people, not thinking of himself. The more a son sacrifices without thinking of himself, the more grateful the father becomes, and the more the brothers rejoice in the fact that he treated them without thinking of himself and crossed the valley of death. This undoubtedly becomes a condition for deeper connections and greater pride.

The life of a true filial son is a life that represents the parents. The goal we desire is the same as God's goal. Because it is a path to find the object of God's love, after we become the object before God and receive God's love, if we open the way for others to receive God's love, then that person becomes closer to God than anyone else. Also, if through us, we bring nations and peoples that were far from God closer together for the sake of our brothers, then that person will undoubtedly enter a position where they can be loved and honored more than anyone else by those people.

Therefore, here, we speak of having the heart of parents, using the body of a servant, shedding tears, blood, and sweat for humanity, the earth, and heaven. Why? Because God has done so. Because God has replaced history with tears, sweat, and blood, we, as the objects of His love, must be able to repay that love. In repaying, rather than going for Him, we should go the path He must go. This is the path we must take, and you must understand this. It is a path where we must go while shedding tears, and even while shedding blood. If you truly understand that the father has wandered for 6,000 years shedding tears and blood, then to live a true filial life towards that father, it is natural that I must represent the appearance of that father.

Because God is everywhere, we must recognize the historical foundation where God sheds tears and blood. Whether we go to this village, this mountain, or the fields, we must think that God's traces of tears and blood are left everywhere. No matter where we go, we have come here to experience our father's traces of tears and to offer a resolution of indemnity, gathering our hearts to fulfill the duty of filial piety.

Whether the place you stand is a city or a rural area, it is fine. If you can meet just one person from that village, you must recognize that there is a trace of God's tears in that one person, and that the father's footsteps stop there. If you can be someone who can hold that individual and cry for them to offer a resolution of indemnity, then you can become a child of heaven. You must have the heart to love that one person from the position of an elder brother, to shed tears and sympathize in place of the father; only then will heaven move.

When you bring them before the father, even if you suffer, you must clean them up and dress them nicely so that the father can see the son he has found and rejoice in holding and loving him. You must have the heart that wants to become someone who can see that and be happy.

Now that you know your parents, know God, and know God's love, how busy do you think it is to consider that there are many people in this world who do not know love and whom parents must find? It is our duty to rise up busily and help them meet their parents.

Therefore, we must not only make the people of America the sons and daughters of God but also fulfill our responsibility to go as far as southern Africa and make those people the sons and daughters of God. If we cannot do that, it is our duty to at least set the condition that we have done it with the tears we shed and the blood and sweat we poured out in love for them.

To accomplish this important task, we must now arm ourselves anew in America and quickly go east, west, north, and south. We must hurry to the end and fulfill our responsibility to find those sons and daughters and bring them before God, just as we receive love and gratitude from Him. Not only that, but we must extend our hands to the entire world to do this work. If we have the heart to sacrifice anything for this work, the more we have that heart, the more God will bless us; He will not punish us. He will be pleased, not saddened.

If we consider the mortality rate in America to be 1 in 100, with a population of 220 million, how many is that? 2.2 million people die each year. How vast is that loss? If we think about it, isn't it God's heart to want to save 2.2 million even if it means sacrificing a few thousand who understand His will? If we consider the world's population to be 3.6 billion, even if one person dies among every hundred, that means 36 million people die each year. Now, would God say, "Hey, you guys take a break. Rest"? No, God would want to say to those who are running, "Do more. Run faster."

Just as God has wandered madly for His lost sons and daughters, we must also be willing to take on responsibilities beyond God to find our brothers, so that God can have a little rest. We are standing in such a position. God desires that you take more interest in America than He does, and that you take interest in America on His behalf. Isn't that what God wants? If you feel that this is not just words but a reality, then it cannot be taken lightly.

Who has made this seriousness arise? It has arisen because of God and because of our brothers; it has become serious because of myself.
This is not it. You must understand that the path we take is good regardless of how we go, and that the 220 million American citizens are calling us with a loud voice. I wish that America would become a day like morning, but it has become evening, evening. So, isn't there a destiny to go before the sun sets? This is our urgent situation. If one thinks, "Oh, I'm tired, let the sun set..." then that person cannot be someone who bears such responsibility. We must go before the sun sets.

We are in the position of being the only matchmaker of God's love. Therefore, we must understand that God needs me and America needs me. Is that right, everyone? "Yes." Until now, it may not have been certain, but now we must clearly understand this. For this reason, the path that the people of the world take and the path we take, the goals that the people of the world desire and our goals are fundamentally different. The people of the world are going for themselves. They think about how America is, how their brothers are, how the world is, how God is... fundamentally different. We must understand that we are different. We must recognize that we are different. Even if I drink a glass of water, it's different; when I eat rice, it's different; when I wear clothes, it's different; everything I see and hear is different.

Ultimately, if we become the matchmaker that connects God's one and only love, we become the matchmaker of the Father and the matchmaker of the Son. What a wonderful thing is this! We become the matchmaker of the Father's love. We must understand this tremendous fact of becoming a matchmaker of love.

When a man and a woman get married in the world, if they have a good matchmaker, they will be grateful to that matchmaker for their entire lives. If we become such a matchmaker and through us, God finds His beloved Son, won't God love me, cherish me, honor me, and praise me every time He loves that person? Moreover, won't that person, their descendants, and their nation also praise me? How amazing is this fact! Furthermore, because we are not only matchmakers but also children of God, if we find them, the God who loves His Son will automatically love me more, even if He says not to love me more.

Therefore, what is the one way that we, members of the Unification Church, can receive love even more? It depends on how much we forget ourselves and establish relationships with God and the children on this earth. This is undoubtedly the condition that allows me to be loved more and to be recognized more before heaven and earth.

If we fail to do this, even though there are many people God needs to find, when we fail to do so, God will want to trample us down. "That wretched fellow!" How much would He hate us? More than hating the world, He would hate us even more. Do you understand that? "Yes." If you know that, then go.

Knowing that I have a debt that I cannot repay, and recognizing the effort of God who found me first... wherever I go, if I have received grace, I must repay it. God tells me not to repay that grace to Him. "Please repay it for your brothers." Therefore, the act of giving a cup of water to the least of these is indeed an act done for God. God prefers that over being treated directly by Him.

We are placed in a position where God can believe in, love, and take pride in us. From this perspective, our goal is to practice God's love and weave together the tears of God's love. Since God's sorrow has grown because of me, we must recognize that we have stood in a position where we can achieve a good path that God can trust.

<Prayer> Beloved Father, today is May 5, 1973. Just the other day was the 20th anniversary of the founding of the association in Korea. Father, I know that May is a historic month where a historical scene changes, where a new opportunity is provided. Father, now let Your love's anchor be lowered on the land of America.

This morning, I contacted my beloved children back home by phone. When I see them thinking of heaven with a longing heart for their parents, I am grateful that I reflect once again on whether we long for heaven more than they long for their parents. 

Father, when I hear the voice saying, "Daddy, Mommy," with tears, how many children on this earth have a heartfelt longing for You, saying, "Come quickly, Daddy, Mommy"? Even if there are many homes, among those homes, how many children call out to God with tears, looking at the rising sun, longing for the image of their Father, and looking at the setting sun, yearning for the heart of their Father? That is the problem. Even if many people may sympathize with the songs sung for their parents, we must realize that in the place where the heart that can call God "Daddy, Mommy" dwells, all of heaven and earth are resonating.

Father! We have come to know that our path and our goal are different. We know the clear path we must take today and tomorrow. Father, who has woven the path of suffering! We know that there is still a path we must take. Even if no one calls us, there is a path we must walk. We have come to understand that You are searching for the children who are asleep, unaware of the world, and that You are spending the night searching for them.
In the midst of the veil of death, I realized that you have come to find us, who are here on this earth, with a heart that is anxious. I understood that we must not become ignorant children before your desired wish. We must think about the fact that even in this night and at this time, you are going through the struggles of a thorny path filled with blood and tears, urging us to take steps forward. Before you call us, we must become babies who can cry out "Father," knowing that even if we fall from a bullet, that moment can stimulate hope and desire in the heart of the Father who looks upon that baby in a world of pitch-black darkness. When I think of such things, I earnestly hope that there may be at least one life here among your children who wishes to become a son or daughter who can call out to the Father with their life on the line.

Father! I have been to Washington for nearly ten days. I have seen various things and met many people. I realized that within the heart with which you blessed America, there is sorrow. When I think that wherever I go, the environment for you to embrace and love this country is not established, I understood that the Father who blessed America has become a lonely Father, and I have come to know the position of a sorrowful Father. Now, as we go to connect with them and establish a relationship, I have met many people, thinking that we must fulfill the mission to leave your connection there.

The more I go, the more I realize that you are a pitiful being. We, who must fulfill the duty of filial piety before the pitiful you, know how pitiful we are. We stand in a difficult position where we cannot fulfill all the responsibilities we must, but because your excessive love is buried here, I realized that you are indeed a pitiful being who wishes to receive comfort through these people.

Now, for us, rather than singing a happy tune of joy day by day, we have a mission to kneel down and seek out the sad brothers, advancing with tears of anguish and cries. When we realize that we must pray for the path of destiny that cannot help but shed tears while looking at us, we must go with gratitude, knowing that a new hope can be left in the heart of the Father through us.

No matter what harsh trials come before us, we must endure while thinking of God. We must not become hesitant steps before the hope of tomorrow. I have come to know that we must carry the footsteps of strong, brave, and valiant heavenly soldiers. Father! Until 1977 and 1978, please remember this path that we must lead the children along. I earnestly hope and desire this.

To your young children in Korea, and to the groups of unification scattered across Japan and the world, if there are those who look up and shed tears toward the land of Belvedere, or toward the western sky or the eastern sky, please repay them a millionfold. Oh heaven, I earnestly wish for you to manifest and allow us to reveal that you are alive.

Through 1973, Father, please send a new flame to this land. I earnestly hope and desire that you create a foundation to unfold your will, even by mobilizing countless ancestors in the spirit world.

Father, it was not a path that someone called for us to take. It was not a path that someone waited for us to walk.
