Today and I

Today, I would like to talk about "Today and I."

Just as there are changes in the seasons, everything undergoes change. 

Looking around Belvedere now, we truly feel that it is a wonderful spring season. Spring is a season that everyone loves. Winter and spring are distinctly different seasons. While spring, summer, and autumn naturally connect, there is a stark difference between winter and spring. Therefore, I believe that the time when our hearts and lives undergo significant changes is precisely when winter and spring intersect.

When spring arrives, you see various plants sprouting new buds. This signifies that spring is the time of change for all living things. Furthermore, we also see flocks of migratory birds appearing anew as the seasons change. In spring, we witness the blooming of flowers.

Thus, spring is a season when all things boast their best. We, too, have a deep desire to feel this spring season according to our environment.

On May 64, 1973, at the Belvedere training center, when we think of this spring season, we realize that it is not just a matter of saying, "Spring has come. Spring is a good season." We must consider that to reach this wonderful season, we have gone through a process of suffering different from ordinary seasons. When we compare the season of winter to spring, we must recognize that winter appears as a period of great trials that eventually passes.

The season of winter is seen as the maximum season that suppresses and restrains all vital forces. Therefore, spring feels like a season of change where what has been suppressed and oppressed bursts forth all at once. Similarly, we see changes occurring every time the four seasons change throughout the year. But is this seasonal change only present in nature? No, it is not. We can glimpse this four-season change even within a single day. Morning corresponds to the spring season, daytime symbolizes summer, evening symbolizes autumn, and night can be seen as winter.

When asked whether morning or evening is better, most people say morning is better. Why is that? Because the night, which symbolizes darkness, has covered everything, and after going through the process of welcoming a new morning, morning feels more precious and stimulating to us. Various birds and people also appear in a hopeful and joyful manner in the morning, and the mood of the morning can influence the entire day's activities of a person. Therefore, if the mood is good in the morning, the day's mood will also be good. Morning feels good because we rest and wake up.

Just as there is a spring season in a day, we also know that there are times in a person's life that correspond to the spring season. As you know, adolescence and youth correspond to the spring season of life. Following that, there are the stages of young adulthood, middle age, and old age. We walk the path of spring, summer, autumn, and winter.

When we observe exercise, we know that when we want to start exercising from a state of rest, we must exert effort. We must go through a process of exerting energy to begin exercising smoothly and in order. When we start exercising, it may be difficult at first, but as we continue, it becomes easier. Eventually, when we reach a peak, we will find ourselves moving forward. This follows a similar process to the four seasons.

When we consider all things going through such processes, we cannot help but see that the same applies to human history. When we view it this way, we must answer whether there was indeed a spring season for humanity, who is meant to embrace the ideal world created by God. The answer is, "Ah! No." Why is that? Because of the fall. The fall indicates that humanity has missed the opportunity to experience a spring season in the historical era or in the world of God's creation.

So, when is the time necessary to meet the spring season, like the winter season? It is the period of growth. According to our principles, the time of growth within the realm of results is a period of trials, corresponding to the winter season. Because the spring season has not appeared in the human world, the realm of results remains in a state of trials. We can say that the fallen human history of today seeks to transcend the realm of results.

Ultimately, why do we have suffering, wars, and trials in human history or the human world? It is because we are in a process that must overcome the realm of results globally; in other words, to reach our original spring season, we must overcome such trials.

The night period is not a time when good things are active; rather, it is a time when bad things are active, and it is not a time when ideal forms appear, but rather when opposing forms manifest. To have gone through this process is different from the usual position. As we approach the peak of winter and get closer to spring, we must think that there will be a time to transcend.

When does the morning sunlight begin to greet me? When the clock strikes twelve and midnight passes, the morning sunlight begins to come toward us. Who knows that time? It is not an exaggeration to say that there is no one in the world who knows that time, the time when one can say, "This is the real time." If there is someone who can say they have fully obtained spring, they must have experienced the entire spring season from the beginning to the end. Only then can we say they have truly welcomed spring.

We do not clearly know when spring transitions to summer, or when summer transitions to autumn, or when autumn transitions to winter. We know that history turns and passes like a wheel, even when we are not aware of it or do not pay attention. From this perspective, we have understood that human history passes through the realm of results, that is, the night period. Therefore, winter must pass for spring to come.

We must know what season we are in. 

Today, when we say that this world goes through such processes, even within the realm of world destiny, each of your individual destinies is entirely different. Your personalities are all different. Some are positive, while others are negative. Some have both positive and negative traits. There are various forms mixed together. There are people who are cold, warm, cool, and gentle... There are all kinds of people. A person who is cold like winter must go through a trial process that is so severe that it seems pitiful to ordinary people in order to transcend to spring. While some people dance with joy, others may possess abundant wealth and can boast about themselves, and there are various kinds of people.

You must know what season you correspond to. A person with a personality that corresponds to autumn should not say, "Oh, I like summer." They should not go in the opposite direction. No matter how hard they try, they cannot succeed. A person corresponding to autumn must overcome and transcend winter, no matter how difficult it may be. Just as individual destinies are like this, we must recognize that many nations in the world are in similar realms of destiny.

The universe is in motion. Everything is in motion, which is why it is turning. Therefore, while it is difficult at the start, it becomes easier once you begin, and while it is difficult to climb up, if this is the autumn season, crossing over the peak is the winter season. The same principle applies. The rise and fall of all nations in the world also develop or regress according to this principle, as we know through historical eras.

Thus, when we look at history or the movements of the world, we cannot simply conclude that it is an unhappy world. The question is, where does the problem lie? It lies in what season we are in. This is all we need to know. When we speak of a country, we must understand what seasonal process our country is going through. Therefore, the issue is that we must overcome whatever challenges arise.

Thus, we must think about what relationship we have with time and ourselves. If this is the spring season, how wonderful it would be if my destiny were in a position similar to the spring season. If my personality is like that of spring, I cannot help but love spring.

That is why everyone has different preferences for seasons. Some people really love spring, some love summer, some love autumn, and some love winter. Not everyone loves only spring. 

The present age is a time when the temperate civilization and the polar civilization are colliding. 

When you observe the stages of civilization development, you can see that it requires a certain process to manifest in any form. Civilization must sprout through the spring season, pass through the summer and autumn seasons, and then develop into a cosmic spring civilization through the winter season.

The spring season can be said to correspond to the youth period. The youth period is a time when everything is expressed. Therefore, if you look at the youth stage, everyone seeks to establish a relationship with everything, and there is no one who is not a poet, no one who does not engage in literature, and everyone wants to connect emotionally with the universe. This time is like the adolescent season, the spring season.
Moreover, adolescent girls laugh even when they see dry leaves rolling in the wind. The reason why the adolescent period, which is a spring season, is so good is that they can harmonize with everything. For this reason, the emergence of culture can be said to come from the environmental conditions in which people can completely empathize with and yearn for everything in their hearts. We can understand that new civilizations go through processes similar to those of summer, autumn, and winter seasons, moving toward a new civilization sphere.

When we think of past civilizations, we can see that their origins are mostly connected to the tropical zone. Civilizations such as Egyptian, Indian, Babylonian, and Chinese all originated from areas close to the tropics. We see that these origins are the civilizations that mature and move on.

Now, what civilization that originated from the tropical zone is currently in what civilization sphere? We can feel that it is situated in the temperate civilization sphere. Centered around the equator, within the latitudes corresponding to 23 degrees north to 38 degrees north, we understand that the temperate zone is intertwined with the limits where the sun moves back and forth. Most countries that boast of their civilization, such as England and the United States, are generally in the temperate zone.

Then, what season does this temperate zone correspond to? We can glimpse that it is entering a civilization sphere corresponding to the autumn season, not the spring season. As it gradually rises, it corresponds to the winter season, and what we encounter next is the polar civilization centered around the Soviet Union. This polar civilization collides with the temperate civilization. Therefore, we can name communism as a polar civilization that originated from a polar civilization area symbolizing the north, winter.

To be a seed with the vitality to overcome winter, this polar civilization acts as a brake on the advancement of the temperate civilization. It is taking an offensive approach. Therefore, this era is like the harvest season of human history. You must understand that today's democratic world corresponds to the harvest season of human history.

So, what is the issue here? The question is whether there are fruits with vitality that have borne fruit in this autumn season. If it has become a seed with vitality, that seed can bring about new changes in the spring season once it overcomes winter. It can bring forth life. Right now, because the wind is blowing from the north, the Christian civilization of the democratic world can all lose their leaves and branches can become bare and die. We can see that this is the time to overcome trials faced with such harsh conditions.

Then, what remains here is whether there is a completely matured seed with the vitality to overcome this winter season. Only such seeds remain. Even when you look at the seeds of pine or cedar trees, the arrival of winter causes them to break through their hard shells. Thus, it can create conditions that allow life to grow. Winter also acts to unify life. Winter is the time when life is most condensed. However, when it passes over the peak, it expands infinitely.

So, are there seed-like people within today's Christian civilization? Are there beings like seeds? Are there individuals like seeds, families like seeds, and nations like seeds? What do you think? "Yes." What is the "yes"? Therefore, when it is said that it has become such a seed, it must possess the confidence and vitality to say, "Come, communism, if you dare. I will swallow you whole." It means we must not be defeated by communism. Are there such people among Christians? "No!" What is that? Where are you? "Yes." Really? Looking at your eyes, it seems you lack confidence.

Now, regardless of how cold the winter is, is there anyone who can say, "I can melt this winter"? Do you have that strength? "Yes." That will be a time when, at some point in the winter season, you will be able to say "Ah!" and get over it. You may not know it, but spring will surely come, because no matter how cold it is, spring will eventually come from afar.

Some people may die after crossing this peak. Some seeds may…. Perhaps you are like that? "No." (Laughter) There may be some who, after crossing the peak, go a little way and then die. When spring comes and the owner is ready to plow the field and sow seeds, at that time, such seeds may die. Would you like to be such a seed? "No." There can be such people.

Seeds that are not held in the hands of the owner cannot find a place to bear new good fruits. Therefore, without someone moving them, there cannot be a new change in the environment to establish the connections of life. You must clearly understand this. So, do you want to be planted through the environment of change? "Yes." Yes? Really? "Yes."

When you plant seeds, do you wash them with clean water and plant them in a place as bare as sand, or do you just throw them in a dirty place? "In a dirty place." Why is that? The Unification Church is also a seed. It is like one seed. What kind of seed is this? It is a seed to create a nation. To create a nation, a new seed family must be planted. It just does what it is told.

What we need to learn and practice
This 100-day training session is planned to continue indefinitely. It is intended to last for a year. Therefore, new members, even if you are newly arrived, you will not be treated separately from the 100-day trainees. You will eat the same food and follow the same schedule.

The purpose of this 100-day training session is to establish a new tradition. I will now explain the content that led to the start of this training session. We must revise, correct, and change all the traditions that the American church and American members have regarding the Unification Church. This training session was initiated with the purpose of achieving that goal. As part of that strategy, we organized a mobilization team. And this training session was also started to fulfill that purpose.

Thus, from the highest executives down, we must engage in the movement to establish a new tradition. That is the leader's thought. So, I first appointed Mr. Young-woon and Mr. Sang-cheol, who were missionaries here, as the leaders of the mobilization team. And I have also included all the members who have been in the Unification Church the longest, including those at the headquarters, into the mobilization team.

May 7, 1973 (Monday), Belvedere Training Center. 
* This message was given to the 100-day trainees, and the title was assigned by the editor.

Until now, the district representatives have been active, but they should not continue to operate with past notions. They must innovate into a new system. Therefore, I have included all district leaders under the mobilization team. This means that local leaders must absolutely not act individually. When the mobilization team leader goes out, they must operate under the complete management of the mobilization team leader. That is how it has been done until now.

Thus, we have established a direction to cooperate with each other and unite with the mobilization team. However, there have been many side effects and various problems. Now, we have come to realize to some extent how we should proceed. It is because we have reached the time to realize that, that we have started this training session. The reason for starting the training session lies there.

Master the lecture techniques during the training period
As I see it, the district leaders here are not yet equipped with the ability to lead a state in America. Therefore, since there are not enough people, I have asked each district and church to send three people who can become successors. Those people are the ones attending this training session.

So originally, when starting this training session, I instructed that six principle lectures should be conducted over 40 days. Originally, just like in Korea, the principle lectures should be detailed, and you must listen to three of them in detail. You must listen to the same lecture three times. Why is that? Because if you do not listen that way, when you go out to the local areas and receive various questions, you will be caught off guard. If you do not know the details and do not listen that way... However, if you listen and leave a record, even if you cannot answer questions at that moment, you can refer back to it later and be equipped to answer in the future.

Next, you must listen to the intermediate level at least twice. For example, if the lecture on the principle of creation took six hours, you must listen to the content in three hours and have two lectures. After that, even if it takes six hours, you must listen to at least once in a two-hour lecture, which is why I said to conduct six lectures. By doing so, you will listen to the same lecture six times, and it will be impossible for you not to understand the principles. You cannot not understand the content.

Then, based on what you have listened to in detail, the second time, and the third time, you must think for yourself and develop your own lecture techniques. Why must you do that? Because the environment and the audience differ, you must have the ability to respond flexibly. Therefore, during this period, you must take at least three tests. One test will be on the detailed content you listened to, the next will be on the intermediate level, and the final stage will require at least one test to assess your scores. Those who score well on these lectures will be planned to be sent out to the local areas. Based on their study results, test scores, and your evaluations—meaning your recommendation that this person is suitable for future life and as a church leader in external relations—they will be selected, and meetings will be held to evaluate and send out one-third or twenty people, depending on the number.

This is the movement we are undertaking. First of all, as a leader of the Unification Church, it is essential to know the principles. Currently, those who are working out there have been going in their own ways, listening to the principles several times, which is why we have not established a standard process. This has led to many people being dropped out. Therefore, now, wherever you go in the country, you must conduct uniform lectures and raise uniform activity results. If the activity results do not rise uniformly, then there will be a problem that requires changing the educational system. This time, twenty people went out from here, but you should not think that they are perfect.

To become a leader, of course, you must give lectures, but you must also pioneer, so you must gain experience in economic issues and social activities. Until now, what have the district representatives done? They have not focused on evangelism but have been employed, with evangelism being a secondary occupation. If there are any among you who have been employed until now, please raise your hand. That cannot be allowed. This is what I dislike the most. Originally, in 1969 or so, I had assigned people to 38 states. They could not develop because they were engaged in employment. They did not develop, and this is how things have turned out. Therefore, having a job and solving living issues while pioneering means that heaven will not cooperate under those conditions. This is what I think must be completely innovated.

You must also gain experience in economic issues and social activities.
Therefore, in a short period, we must teach the ability to solve economic issues and living problems. That is why we plan to bring in Japanese members to provide that education. So, you must follow what the Japanese members do. If they can achieve those results without being able to speak and while not being accustomed to the living environment of this area, then American members must do even better. That is my belief. You must do better than that.

Currently, Japanese members are earning $80 or $100 a day. If they work for a month, that means they are working. So, if they work for just a week, not even full days, just a few hours over several days, they can solve their living issues for a month. They can earn it. It is very liberating. They are not tied down and do not suffer mental anguish. Until now, they have been constrained by economic issues, but I believe that this will completely break through.

You should sell candles... If possible, you should learn to sell flowers. Why is that? Because flowers, no matter how long they last, do not last more than a week. They last only five days.
The moon, it goes for a year, you know. So that cannot be the standard we deal with.  
197  
From that perspective, this flower selling is something that is indispensable and important in our activities. I think it is a secret key to solving economic problems.  
Even if you have no money at all, that's fine. Even without a penny, if you go to a flower shop and work for just one hour and ask for three flowers, anyone would do that for you. Then you take that and sell it. With that, you can sell ten, a hundred... If you sell like that, you can do it as much as you want.  
If you worked for an hour, then in your spare time, if you sell that and buy more, the economic problem is solved. That way, you won't be threatened in your life. The fact that we can stand in a position where we can disregard living issues becomes a source of great power. So, the second purpose of this training is to create confident individuals in economic activities.  
Next is external activities, competition activities. In external activities, activities that contact individuals, activities that contact the public, activities that contact high-ranking people, activities that contact low-ranking people, this expands the scope. When the first-time participants visit like this, if they sit with high-ranking people, they become shy. Because they have no experience, they make many mistakes.  
Why do I bring you to New York for this kind of education? New York is the leading city in the United States. It is one of the most recognized cities in the world. The level of knowledge is high, and the level of culture is also high. Therefore, if you gain confidence here, you won't be rough anywhere in the country. If you say you trained in New York in the provinces, no one can look down on you. The teacher instructed to hold competitions here every week, so we are currently holding competitions.  
After training in flower selling or candle selling here, you must go to the New York church and receive practical teachings on personal evangelism or overall activities. You need to earn points there to be sent out. The person in charge there must say that this person can be sent out, and only then will they be assigned to the next local area. Until you have the confidence to evangelize confidently, taking responsibility for one person each month, you will not be sent out.  
198  
This is the process the teacher is teaching this time. Naturally, it will take 100 days. 100 days will naturally pass.  
Only skills and performance can be factors for development.  
This time, the members from Europe will start participating from the second round. If their test scores are good, the European members will also participate in this activity. We sent out 20 people from here, and if we don't attract more than 20, this training won't happen. That's why we assigned 30 this time. At least 80 to 100 people need to be trained here at any time. So, good performers will be sent out, and as that happens, it will come back around. I think it will take about three rounds to make a full circle.  
Then, the leaders will train the incoming people in the same way as the training methods here. They will educate the members like that. After training them, when it is said, "This person can be trained as a representative of our nation, a talent needed in America," they will be recommended to come here for training as a principle. If this continues, the state representatives will become like that, and then three or four people will be continuously produced from each state.  
You are here as state representatives now, but do not think that you will go to that state. This time, I went to Washington and designated everyone and assigned them all. Without skills and performance, you cannot develop in the future. Only skills and performance are the factors for your future development. Because you are here, the position of state representative is vacant, so we will fill it one by one among these 20 people. After six months, at least a few people will have their skills and performance gradually increase. If after six months, no one has evangelized, if you can't meet the standard of three people in six months, one person a month, then we will bring in more and train again. We will assign good performers here and bring in those who couldn't perform.

This way, statistics will come out nationwide. Records will be established. This will continue for one or two years. No matter how long someone has been a district leader, if they have no performance, they will come in here. The 20 people assigned this time will compete with the old leaders. If they compete with each other, no matter how long they have been there, those with poor performance will have to come in for training. If they are sent out once, twice, or three times and have no performance, we cannot recognize their qualifications to lead our church. Those people will be sent to business fields or elsewhere.  
By doing this, the leaders of the Unification Church nationwide will become active members standing on the same unified standard. If you go out without studying this time and lose to someone who works hard, you will come back in. Therefore, those who are active on the front lines must always be interested in how the newcomers can perform and improve their results, and they must strive not to lose. If that happens, development will naturally occur.  
This time, as I implement this in the United States, I will also do the same in Japan and plan to establish this system throughout Europe. Until now, it was not possible because there were not enough people. Originally, it means that there should be three times the number of members for someone to become a leader. Because that number was not met, this system could not be established. However, from now on, I plan to unify this plan globally. Do you understand? "Yes." If you have questions about this, feel free to ask. So, how do you think it will be? Do you think it will be good or bad? "I think it will be good."  
It is undeniable that by giving principle lectures, we represent our church, then we solve economic problems through economic activities, and then we solve social issues... That is sufficient. After that, I intend to take outstanding individuals from here and teach them about victory lectures and unification thought. Consequently, the number of capable leaders will gradually increase. No matter how early someone entered here, if they lack skills, they will not be recognized. I intend to recognize based on skill standards. No matter how much they know the principles and chatter, if they have no performance, it won't work. At any time, skills and performance are the only criteria for recognition. Do you understand? A More Valuable Path
I hope this gathering is meaningful for all of you who have returned after your hard work across the country. Since this is the third time you have gathered here, I hope this meeting serves as a good opportunity for you to set a new path and resolve anew. Today, I would like to briefly speak to you about "A More Valuable Path." I will discuss this topic.
Value is determined by motivation, relative conditions, and purpose.
No one wants to take a path that results in loss. When considering all the relationships and circumstances that connect me to everything, it becomes a matter of whether this is beneficial or detrimental to oneself. Therefore, our daily thoughts revolve around seeking benefits and finding more valuable outcomes.
Then, where does the more valuable path begin? It cannot start apart from me. Ultimately, the issue is that the person known as "I" must be the subject or motivation. It goes without saying that when we face a beneficial path, a more valuable path, we feel joy. That is what we humans are.
May 15, 1973 (Tuesday), Belvedere Training Center.
236   A More Valuable Path
Now, when we consider the issue of value, we must think about where a more valuable path can begin. When we look at good things, it is determined by whether the motivations are good, whether the relative conditions are good, and whether the purpose is good; these three conditions decide it. In other words, it is determined when the counterpart completely unites.
To say something is good means it adds a plus to me. And to say something is bad means it presents a minus event to me. Good things...
is always something we want to combine for a long time, while we want to quickly dispose of and separate from bad things after having combined them. 

When we look at our individual daily lives, how do people feel about others they like? When the events of their past or the motivations of their lives are similar, they can come together. Then, if there is a relative relationship, that is, if a man is with a man or a woman is with a woman, they can relate to each other and like each other. Furthermore, when their desired goals are the same, they can continue to like each other. In human life, we can summarize the fact that people come together and separate due to these three factors: the past, the present, and the future are all concentrated in the concepts of motivation, relative concepts, and goal concepts.

For a better value to be established, good people and goodness itself do not change. It does not change! As time goes on, it shines brighter, and it does not diminish or retreat; this is the concept of goodness. It is the path of goodness. This relative concept must be paired with a greater purpose, and one must pursue a more valuable purpose to become one. If that purpose is achieved, what will happen? The purpose itself must be developed and expanded; the goal must be realized as a single result. The conclusion is that we must end it and see the conclusion before starting something new.

Even when we speak, there is a motivation behind the words. There must be a counterpart to speak to. There is always a purpose in speaking. If that purpose is achieved and we continue to speak, it becomes stimulating or does not concern us. It remains just a passing matter. 

When a purpose is achieved, it should not remain as just that achieved purpose. If we do not establish a new motivation centered around that achieved purpose, there will be no development. We can conclude that a higher dimension cannot be established from this. Ultimately, we can conclude that the first achieved purpose appears as the material for the next motivation, and only through this can development and good results be pursued. Principles of the interaction and development of motivation, relative conditions, and purpose

The more you repeat the principle lectures, the more valuable they become.

One of the drawbacks for Americans is that they do not want to repeat the same thing. I know this is the temperament of Americans. If I become a sinner at that time, is it the same as a sinner in America? No. It's different. You cannot imagine such a place. When you are so hungry that you go out and work hard to eat, and if you die while eating, you take food from that person's mouth. That's how it is. Do you understand that? Seeing such things, the teacher thought, 'Hmm, even if I have to do a hundred times or a thousand times more than this, I will go.' You have to digest everything like that.

Even in the communist prison, I was the top laborer. Every year, I received awards, and Mr. Moon received awards. I cannot lose to the world of Satan. No matter how severe the persecution I faced, I stood tall.... 'When you give me an award, you must greet me; even in prison, the warden must greet me.' I thought of such things. That is necessary. No matter how much you are in prison, you must feel the mission to subdue Satan and come back.

That is why God walks this path with me. Because God cannot do without a person like me, He raises someone like me to do His work. While others all perish, I am no different now. What is that? I did not yield in my heart, in my spirit. It's the same here in America. When I decide to do something, I will do it, no matter who opposes me. If I die, I will fight fiercely even in death. You must know that.

What the teacher wants to do will happen. Once I decide to do it, I will do it. Once I start, there is no way to retreat. It’s either die or live.

In that sense, you have met wrongly. You have met wrongly. "No." 'Young people are all playing and dancing, doing whatever they want, what is this?' You might want to. "No." You can't say 'no'.... You know that well. (laughs) But if no one does this work, the universe, this world will perish. A huge snowball is rolling. This is rolling, and someone must put on the brakes. To do that, you must sacrifice.

Those who transcend death and life become friends with God.
You young people like to dance while riding on the rolling big globe, saying, 'Oh, how nice! Oh, how nice! Oh, how nice!' You are doing this. Soon, you will not even know when you will be crushed.... That is the situation. Singing and dancing, how fun is this? It seems like the whole world is for me.

However, just go a little further. The world is destined to be crushed all at once. Will you just watch that, or will you try to stop it even if it means dying? Then you will die. If one person dies, there are others who can die, and if ten people die, a hundred can die, and if a hundred die, a thousand can die, and if a thousand die, ten thousand can die, and if ten thousand die, a hundred thousand can die.... It can increase by hundreds of times; without a nation or organization that can prepare for death, this world cannot be saved, that is the teacher's thought.

Therefore, you must be able to compete to die. Just like the disciples of Jesus, you must not run away from the place of death. If you cannot be the one who says, 'I will die first,' you cannot save the world. You must know that. What will you do? Will you not be like the disciples of Jesus? "Yes." Those disciples were the ones who were defeated in the face of Satan's fearful environment. They said they believed well, but Satan took all twelve of them in one fell swoop and threw them away. But what about Jesus? Satan tried but failed.

That is why the wise thing was that even while dying, one could resurrect again.
It's said that I tried to find a way and die. That's what greatness is. You all are the same. If we can't achieve it in my generation, we must pave the way for our descendants to surely achieve it. We must understand that those who die after laying down the path of goodness become ancestors who can inherit the history of goodness.

Now, did Jesus lose when he was attacked by Satan? "No, he didn't." God, who is scarier than Satan, fights on our behalf. That's the issue. You must understand this. God fights for justice. In the end... you need to know this.

Have you ever thought, "When will I be defeated? When will I be broken?" Have you thought about that? Even if my fingers get cut off, or I die from being cut, or if I get shot all at once, it can be possible. "My life was that, my whole being was that, my death was due to that, and my life was because of that..." Such a person transcends death and life. Because God transcends death and life, such a person becomes a friend of God. That's who God is. Because He transcends death and life, a person who goes to that place, whether they die or live, becomes a friend of God. Yes, have you become a friend of God? "Yes." So, those who live with God as their friend should not be petty. Do you want to become friends with Satan? "No." Not only do we want to be friends with God, but we also want to make God our Father. That's even more wonderful. We want to make God ours.

You need to understand this. Throughout history, many of our ancestors were like a cell of God, like a finger. When that gets cut, wouldn't God feel that pain? When you have children, if those children die, it hurts more than your own death. It would be better to cut off your own hand. God has endured such pain for thousands of years and is still bravely advancing for tomorrow's victory. Isn't He our Father? Am I not the one who has inherited that Father's tradition? So, what should I do? It's a natural question. For the final victory, at the forefront...

**The Importance of Training**
If you put your life on the line, you will succeed in anything.

Now, you all are like that, but do you get tired after a year? Do you get tired after two years? Do you get tired after ten years? Do you get tired after twenty years? How many years will it take before you get tired? Think about it. How many years will you get tired? "I will never get tired." Never? Really? "Yes." I can't believe you. Just a little bit of something happens, and you...

You need to understand it as fun: "I was born for this, so this is my fate! I can't live without this." You should think that way. This is a fun thing, and you need to discover joy, happiness, and excitement here.

The teacher started this work even before you were born. Looking at you, most of you are in your thirties... I have done a lot of work. I think there is even more to do than before. There is more to do. That's why I don't want to boast about today. If there is something to boast about, I think about how to invest that in tomorrow's fight. The road ahead is busy. Do I look tired? "No." I'm not tired. Even more so, as time goes on, it becomes more stimulating, more powerful, and more wonderful. You should feel that, not be tired or anything...

So, look at yourselves. Who set the standard for your own happiness, saying, "I must live like this to be happy. If I live like this, I will be unhappy"? That has nothing to do with me! You should think that way. Because I didn't set it, it has nothing to do with me.

My right to happiness is something I will establish from now on. "Being hungry, struggling, and suffering is our happiness." Then that is happiness. If there are people who say that, will they lose the world or conquer the world? They will say that dying quickly is happiness. Why? Because there is a spiritual world.

Look. If the spiritual world is better than the earthly world, (writing on the board) if the spiritual world is structured like this, when you compare this with that, which is bigger? This is the spiritual world. If we live for a hundred years, and if living on this earth is longer, then think about it: is living longer happiness or living shorter happiness? Which is bigger? If you enter the spiritual world, who got there first? Who entered the spiritual world first? The one who got there even a day earlier is better. It's the same. The one who joined the Unification Church even a day earlier is the senior, right? Isn't that so?

That's why living long isn't necessarily good. Before I grow old, after going through the path of restoration in my youth, when I am still fresh, when friends and companions can sympathize with me, entering the spiritual world as a wonderful person is happiness. Think about that. Isn't that unhappy?

Therefore, whatever it is, you must put your life on the line. If you do that, you will surely succeed. If you do it, you will succeed even if you don't want to. God, who loves you even more, thinks, "I must make him succeed quickly because I don't know when he will die." If He can't do that and you die and come to the spiritual world, won't God feel sorry? Parents feel that way. If a loving child can't have what they want or need, parents feel regret. It's the same.

God is the Father, and I am the son, yet I am saying I will do something absurd. Even if I shouldn't do it, if I put my life on the line and say, "I do this for my mother and father," and if I do it without knowing I will die, wouldn't the parents want to help with all their might? It's the same. Parents go ahead of their children and take responsibility for everything. Isn't that so? If it's for oneself, then it shouldn't be done, but because it's for the parents, they can't sleep at night and will do it. Because there is that condition of doing it for God, for the Father, for the parents...

Parents are weak in love. They must understand that they cannot be strong in front of their children in love.

That's why when the teacher starts doing something, he forgets to eat, forgets to sleep, and gets intoxicated by it. He thinks only of that and works day and night. In that case, what if the teacher dies? God has all the calculations. He has to cooperate with this.

Also, look. Now, when you look at the Unification Church, some people say it's a small group, but that's not true. Look. Even Jesus couldn't find ten people, or even three people, who would die with him during his lifetime. Confucius, Buddha, and no one else had a foundation like the Unification Church while they were alive. But today, the teacher has a global foundation while still alive. And it's global. Did Jesus do that? The teacher is someone who succeeded more than any sage while still alive. Isn't that right? "Yes." Even looking at that, it's worth believing. You need to understand how wonderful this meaning is.

If we had just one nation, think about what would have happened. How many... how many years would we have moved the world? Would this world be a problem? Would it not be? "It wouldn't." You need to understand that. That's why there may not be anything more wonderful than this... Would the teacher not have thought as much as you? No matter how much I think, there seems to be no way. Because there is only this way, I am playing this game. I am someone who has thought more than you. Before you go, I have already gone. I have been everywhere.

This path is a wonderful path. Moreover, if you were born a man, it's a path worth taking once, and even more so, if you were born a woman, it's a game worth trying. If you try it, there will be no regret. Whether born a man or a woman, it is the same for both.

To overcome the standard of character judgment, you must subdue Satan.

What is character judgment? Satan attacks individuals, families, nations, and the world. In that attack, you must be able to say, "Even if you attack individuals, it won't work. Even if you attack families, it won't work. Even if you attack nations, it won't work. Even if you attack the world, it won't work." This must be the case, whether it's day or night...

Do you not think about this? You are only thinking about moving forward, saying "It's forward," and putting in your strength, but if you get hit, you will advance even if you just stay still. What you hit will fall behind instead. If you are trying to go this way and you are pushed to go that way, if you end up jumping forward, then you will retreat. When Satan persecutes, it is not that you retreat; rather, when Satan touches you, you advance instead, so you must make Satan understand that "touching that is harmful."

If you do this a few times, it will be said that there is nothing left to test, nothing left at all. There is a saying, right? (laughs) Is that true? Do you want that? "Yes." Can you just stay still? Can you just stay still? "No." That's why you need to train. You need to train.

Even if Satan's cunning methods that led our ancestors to ruin are applied to me, I must stand in the position of a victor who can subdue Satan without being drawn into it. Only then can I become a recognized victor in character judgment by God.

God, who has gone through all historical eras, will say, "Looking at you, hey! You resemble me. When Abraham failed in his offering, when Moses failed, when Joseph and Zechariah failed in the time of Jesus, I was unaffected, and seeing that you are also unaffected, you resemble me." That must be the case. When that happens, character perfection is achieved. When that happens, you can become a great figure who can judge humanity. In other words, you can not only surpass character judgment but also establish the standard of judgment as God's representative. There must be that standard, right? Today, you succeeded, but in the past, you failed; that is not the case. Success is the same in the past, today, and tomorrow. God succeeded in the past, is succeeding today, and can succeed tomorrow, so we must be the same.

Does God think, "Hey, Satan, come if you want!" or does He say, "Oh, don't come, don't come!"? Does God say to Satan, "If you want to attack, come!" or does He say, "That's enough, stop attacking"? What does God say? "Come if you want..."

Shouldn't you be the same? "America, come! Commander of this state, come! You will melt in my hands." Shouldn't you say that? "The nation, come!" That's what you should do. Right? "Yes." Is that really true? "Yes." That's how it should be. But if you say, "Oh no, I'm scared! How can I meet the police? How can I meet the police chief? Oh, I don't want to. You go!" (laughter) As a person in charge, saying, "I can't make money, so you earn it all," that kind of attitude won't do. What are you going to do? Are you going to do this? (expressing with actions) Are you going to do this? What is it? Is it forward, is it stopped, or is it retreating? Is it retreating, is it stopped, or is it advancing? Among these three types, which one are you? You belong to one of these three types. Which one are you? "It's advancing." Is that just talk? Is that the reality? "Yes." Until now, it hasn't been the reality, but from now on, it must become the reality.

That's why you must have the conviction, "Let's see the powers in this state! Let's see the wealthy businessmen! I will not lose." "Yes, even if they come at night, okay, even if they come while I'm sleeping, whenever they come... I must be ready to jump out even if I'm in the restroom." That's how it should be. You shouldn't say, "Hey, wait a minute!" when someone calls you while you're eating or resting. You should say, "Yes, I've been waiting for you to come." You should be ready to jump out even if you're sleeping. That's how it should be. Right?

"Satan, whether you control some foolish person or some talented person, or whether you control some material, come! If you come, I can digest it all." That is the confidence you should have.

That's why the teacher's character, no matter where he goes or what sports event he attends, will shout, "Hey!" and will come after that. Even when he goes there... even when he goes to the mountains, he should go to the highest place first, shed tears, and pray. He must be first in everything. When he gets on any platform to speak, he must do it while sweating. He must have the mindset that "I will sweat a lot, and I will bleed a lot; I am more passionate than anyone else."

You must walk around for 24 hours until your feet wear out. You must try it for a week. You must do it without sleeping or eating.

The fastest way to be number one is to do what others cannot do.

What others do, they all do, so there is a way to be number one by doing what others cannot do. That is the only fast way. Other things, they are doing best, so you must prepare to hit them in another area. They all have money and power. Therefore, what is left for us is only ideology. Since they dislike ideology, if you become number one here, who will break? They will break. They cannot fast. That's why I want to be number one. They cannot go out on the street and sweat while shouting, so I am number one; they cannot sell flowers, so I am number one; they cannot pull a cart, so I am number one; they cannot dig the ground, so I am number one. There are countless things I can do.

If there are people in difficulty, I will go out on the street and campaign to raise money and bring it to them. That's something they cannot do.

I do not boast about being good at one thing. They can do dozens or hundreds of things that they cannot do; who is better? Have you felt that your shoes will have holes in a few months? That's how it should be. A person who does what others cannot do is the one who is truly good. Isn't that right?

What weapons does Satan use? You must cut off all the weapons that Satan uses. You must sever them. Yes, the teacher is a heartless person. He cuts off even his mother. When she came to visit him in prison, shedding tears, he chased her away. He does not want to see a petty mother who cries and feels sad for her son. He welcomes the tears of encouragement to fight more for the world... I have been someone who has done such things. It's the same for you.

If you do not prepare thoroughly so that you will not be caught in Satan's attacking weapons, you cannot appear in the character judgment and cannot win.
You need to understand this.
That is why Jesus said, "Die." This is the thought that even if you die, you won't die. It means that you have overcome everything. When you make such a resolution for God, and if you say that you were born that way and that it aligns with your nature, then there are no trials. That is how you develop. Are you like that? 
If someone is not like that and wishes blessings upon them, they are just serving Satan. God does not bless them. God cannot bless them. If you wish blessings based on such criteria, even if that person falters, that criterion remains in the heavenly realm.
Now, that is why someone who cannot overcome and surpass the historical enemy, Satan, cannot receive God's approval and cannot surpass the standard of personal judgment. What is that standard? You must be better than Jesus. Are you better than Jesus? Are you better than Jesus or not? "I am." (Laughter) You must be better. Jesus died, but He started the conquest of the world by dying, and we must have the belief that we are better than Jesus because we start the conquest of the world while we are alive. Do you understand? "Yes." So always think, "I am better than Jesus."
You must have the belief that "the world is being conquered by my hands, surpassing America and many countries." You must break through Moscow and Beijing. Is that right? "Yes." You must do this (expressing with actions) to surpass the standard of personal judgment.
Time has passed, but shall we continue talking? "Yes." Actually, I did not intend to talk about this today. I am also doing a side job right now. (Laughter) Right now, it is a training session. I ended up here while talking about the training session. I say this, but the teacher does not forget that. You must conclude and align it properly, so you must not forget that. (Laughter) What comes next? What is the third judgment? "The heart judgment and the love judgment." Shall I say it simply in one word or in detail? "In detail." Time is running out. I have no time. Time is limited. Have you truly experienced love? (Recording briefly stops)
Training is needed to make you a global figure.
If our mobilization team goes out with four members to each state and evangelizes 40 people, how many is that? 160 people. If we do that in 50 states, that becomes 8,000 people. When that day comes, we can freely run for Senate and even bring them down. In the future, we must make senators listen to us, and we must make our state leaders listen to us. 
Somehow, we must be equipped with principles and be able to stand up anywhere and do public propaganda when we grab the microphone. Then the Republicans will pull with the right hand, and the Democrats will pull with the left hand. Even if they are not pulled, they will be drawn in. We must not be drawn in and must say, "Come." Otherwise, we cannot save America. In about three years, senators will come to bring the teacher in their cars. Does that sound bad or good? (Laughter) That is how it will be. It has already happened in Korea.
If America is corrupt and the senators do not listen, we can create a party. Don’t all the women here want to become the wives of senators? It is possible. Now, do you want to become a senator as a man? "I want to." You must have the belief that "I will make it happen."
I have met all the famous senators. When I met them, they were nothing. They were the weakest people. The weakest people are afraid of losing elections and are terrified of that. I realized that those who have a confident foundation cannot be weak.
If we become a foundation, will we be confident or not? "We will be." You must think about that. You must not become weak regarding justice. Having such a dream and keeping your mouth shut is just building a nest.
Do not think about that; we must be busy laying our foundation. I will coach that... I want to create a Christian party centered on the Unification Church with all the Christians, Catholics, and Protestants of the world.
We must quickly stop the Communist Party. The Communist Party is coming politically, so our Christian believers must lay such a foundation. The current mainstream church pastors must preach that we need to do such movements to stop the global Communist Party. But they are not preaching that. Therefore, I think it is impossible to do such resistance without laying that foundation, and that is why I am trying to do it.
The separation of religion and politics is just a fallacy that arose to prevent the corruption of Christianity and the papacy during the Middle Ages. What is democracy? It emerged as a new form opposing the corrupt old church based on the Christian revolution. It was created to separate religion and politics, but why should religion and politics be separated? Can you separate God from politics? God is the one who handles this entire world...
That is why we must produce a large number of politicians who are not corrupt to create a heavenly kingdom on earth. Isn’t that right? "That’s right." The phrase "Religion and politics should be separated" is what Satan loves the most.
I am not saying we should do politics right away. If good people, those with such thoughts, increase, the political foundation of this country will naturally shift. If I give an order, and if there are 500,000 of our Unification Church members in America, can those 500,000 follow my order to settle in New York? Yes? "Yes." If I tell Europeans to all immigrate to America, they will immigrate.
So we are filled with hope both inside and out. From a religious perspective, we are being drawn in, and from a political perspective, we are being drawn in. If we cannot work even in this situation, then let us all die. Let us all die. So, do you want to try? Do you want to try? "Yes." What can’t you do! Do you still want to do it? "Yes!" I raised my hand. (Applause)
The teacher has interests in various fields. Last year in Korea, we already started an international religious Olympics. We will blow away the current Olympic games. I believe that the total incident that occurred during the Munich Olympics in Germany last year happened because I took an interest and started it. "You should go down." This is it. From now on, I will go up.
Now, among you, I might send a soccer team to Korea this year. Do you want to lose or win? "We will win." This is how we gradually expand. I plan to expand the events. Soon, it won’t be long before... Do you know why we are doing such activities? All for the purpose...
You may not know, but I think we need to dissolve the United Nations. We need to dissolve the current United Nations. It will become the propaganda stage for the Communist Party in the future. We must prepare for that too. Therefore, it is the teacher's desire that we cannot do without making you global figures. So, is training needed or not? "It is needed." I will give you training that does not exist in the world. At that time, will you say, "Oh, that’s scary!" or will you say, "I will do it"? What will it be? "I will say I will do it." That is how it should be. So, you all resemble me. (Applause)
Now that time has passed, let’s stop here... Today’s training, whether male or female, anyone who has listened to the words today should have organized them in their minds. So, the teacher's request is to evangelize those who can pass and to raise those who can pass.
Everyone who comes can pass all at once here... Then we will create a playground on the Hudson River, and if we set up a playboat, then the world will say, "Hey! Let’s go to training." That time will come. So, with that hope, we must go.
<Prayer> Beloved Father, your children gathered here are now spending three days together. It is now lunchtime. We thank you for allowing us to spend the morning together. May we become your little children who can set up an altar of victory before your earnest desire through all that we have heard and felt. Please do not let us hesitate in front of the path of destiny we must take, but make us heavenly soldiers who advance while welcoming tomorrow seriously and boldly.
Father, I entrust this America to you. I entrust this America to you, so please protect it.
Father, the son standing here is one body. When I think of the path you must take with a longing heart, I am anxious, and even if the visible nature is beautiful, I have a constrained heart that cannot praise you upon seeing it. You know, Father, that it is also your wish to end this year and this life with vitality and a free heart on a day of desire.
Please nurture these people well. We are stepping on the ground where the Puritans who were heading from the East to the West had hoped for more than their desires, and we are able to practice it as a reality, so do not be discouraged but pledge to advance and become sons and daughters who can fulfill a mission worthy of receiving your love and being praised by all nations.
Thank you for being with us in the time that comes and goes, and I ask you to bless this day, and I pray in the name of True Parents. Amen. *
